Please enter your phone number.\");\n  }, []);\n\n  // Voice recognition setup\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (SR) {\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\n      \n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\n        let text = '';\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n          text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\n        }\n        setTranscript(text);\n        \n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) {\n          processVoice(text);\n        }\n      };\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  const processVoice = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = {\n      'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4',\n      'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0'\n    };\n    \n    let processed = text.toLowerCase();\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) {\n      processed = processed.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\b${word}\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\n    }\n    \n    const digits = processed.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    if (digits.length > 0) {\n      const newPhone = (localPhone + digits).slice(0, 10);\n      setLocalPhone(newPhone);\n      onChange(newPhone);\n      \n      if (newPhone.length === 10) {\n        speak(\"Phone number complete. rows={4}\n          style={{\n            width: '100%', padding: '14px 16px',\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n            border: `1px solid ${THEME.accent}40`,\n BuilderUpload: React.FC<Props> = ({ onFileSelect, onProductsExtracted, speak }) => {\n  const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);\n  const [status, setStatus] = useState<'idle' | 'uploading' (!file) return;\n    \n    setUploading(true);\n    setStatus('uploading');\n    setFileName(file.name);\n    speak(`Uploading ${file.name}`);\n    onFileSelect(file);\n\n    const formData = new      const data = await response.json();\n      \n      setStatus('success');\n      onProductsExtracted(data.products || []);\n      speak(\"Portfolio uploaded successfully!\");\n    } catch (err) {\n      setStatus('error');\n      speak(\"Upload failed. Please try again.\");\n    } finally {\n      setUploading(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 20 }}>\n      <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n        <span style={{ fontSize: '2.5em' }}>\ud83d\udcc1</span>\n        <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: '10px 0 5px' }}>Upload Portfolio</h3>\n        <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Upload project photos, floor plans, or documents</p>\n      </div>\n\n      <div\n        onClick={() => !uploading && fileInputRef.current?.click()}\n        style={{\n          border: `2px dashed ${status === 'success' ? accept=\".pdf,.jpg,.jpeg,.png,.docx\"\n          onChange={e => e.target.files?.[0] && handleUpload(e.target.files[0])}\n          style={{ display: 'none' }}\n        />\n\n        {status === 'idle' && (\n          <>\n            <div style={{ fontSize: '3em', marginBottom: 15 }}>\ud83d\udcc1</div>\n            <p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Click to upload portfolio</p>\n            <p style={{ color: '#64748b', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>PDF, Images, Documents</p>\n          </>\n        )}\n\n        {status === 'uploading' && (\n          <>\n            <div style={{       <>\n            <div style={{ fontSize: '2.5em', marginBottom: 15 }}>\u2705</div>\n            <p style={{ color: '#10b981', fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Upload successful!</p>\n            <p style={{    <p style={{ color: '#ef4444' }}>Upload failed</p>\n          </>\n        )}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default BuilderUpload;\nBUILDERUPLOAD\n\necho \"  \u2705 const [otp, setOtp] = useState('');\n  const [companyName, setCompanyName] = useState('');\n  const [profile, setProfile] = useState('');\n  const [products, setProducts] = useState<any[]>([]);\n\n  const synth = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.speechSynthesis : null;\n  \n  const speak = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    if (!synth) return;\n    synth.cancel();\n    const utterance = STEPS.length - 1) setStep(STEPS[idx + 1]);\n  };\n\n  const goBack = () => {\n    const idx = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n    if (idx > 0) setStep(STEPS[idx - 1]);\n    else onBack();\n  };\n\n  const speak={speak}\n          />\n        );\n      case 'dashboard':\n        return <BuilderDashboard companyName={companyName} onContinue={goNext} speak={speak} />;\n      case 'upload':\n        return Complete!</h2>\n            <p style={{ color: '#888' }}>Your builder account is ready.</p>\n            <button\n              onClick={onClose}\n              style={{\n                padding:   >\n              Go to Dashboard\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        );\n      default:\n        return null;\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{\n      position: 'fixed', background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.primary}, ${THEME.secondary})`,\n        borderRadius: 20,\n        width: '100%', maxWidth: 600,\n        maxHeight: '90vh',\n        overflow: 'hidden',\n        border: `2px solid ${THEME.accent}40`\n      }}>\n        {/* Header */}\n        <div style={{\n          padding: '16px 24px',\n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\n          borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.accent}30`,\n          display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center'\n        }}>\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 14 }}>\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\ud83c\udfd7\ufe0f</span>\n            <div>\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Builder  </div>\n          </div>\n          <button\n            onClick={onClose}\n            style={{\n              background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n              border: 'none', color: '#fff',\n              width: 36, height: 36, borderRadius: '50%',\n              cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '1.2em'\n            }}\n          >\n            \u2715\n          </button>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Progress */}\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '10px 24px', gap: 4, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>\n          {STEPS.map((_, i) => (\n            <div key={i} style={{\n              flex: 1, height: 4, borderRadius: 2,\n              background: i <= stepIndex ? THEME.accent : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)'\n            }} />\n          ))}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Back button */}\n        <div style={{ padding: '12px 24px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udcf1 STEP 2: Creating BuilderPhone.tsx...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$BUILDER_DIR/BuilderPhone.tsx\\\" << 'BUILDERPHONE'\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useRef, '#1e3a5f', accent: '#f59e0b' };\\n\\nconst BuilderPhone: React.FC<Props> = ({ phone, onChange, onNext, speak }) => {\\n  const [localPhone, setLocalPhone] = useState(phone);\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    speak(\\\"Welcome builder! Please enter your phone number.\\\");\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  // Voice recognition setup\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (SR) {\\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\\n      \\n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\\n        let text = '';\\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\\n          text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n        }\\n        setTranscript(text);\\n        \\n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) {\\n          processVoice(text);\\n        }\\n      };\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const processVoice = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = {\\n      'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4',\\n      'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0'\\n    };\\n    \\n    let processed = text.toLowerCase();\\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) {\\n      processed = processed.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\\\\\b${word}\\\\\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\\n    }\\n    \\n    const digits = processed.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    if (digits.length > 0) {\\n      const newPhone = (localPhone + digits).slice(0, 10);\\n      setLocalPhone(newPhone);\\n      onChange(newPhone);\\n      \\n      if (newPhone.length === 10) {\\n        speak(\\\"Phone number complete. Click Send OTP to continue.\\\");\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }, [localPhone, onChange, speak]);\\n\\n  const toggleListening = () => {\\n    if (isListening) {\\n      recognitionRef.current?.stop();\\n      setIsListening(false);\\n    } else {\\n      recognitionRef.current?.start();\\n      setIsListening(true);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => {\\n    if (p.length <= 3) return p;\\n    if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`;\\n    return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`;\\n  };\\n\\n  const handleChange = (value: string) => {\\n    const digits = value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n    setLocalPhone(digits);\\n    onChange(digits);\\n  };\\n\\n  const isValid = localPhone.length === 10;\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: 20 }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\\ud83c\\udfd7\\ufe0f</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: 0 }}>Builder Phone Number</h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em', margin: 0 }}>\\n        Say digits like \\\"seven zero three\\\" or type below\\n      </p>\\n\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\\n        <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '1.2em' }}>+1</span>\\n        <input\\n          type=\\\"tel\\\"\\n          value={formatPhone(localPhone)}\\n          onChange={e => handleChange(e.target.value)}\\n          placeholder=\\\"000-000-0000\\\"\\n          style={{\\n            padding: '16px 20px',\\n            fontSize: '1.5em',\\n            fontFamily: 'monospace',\\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n            border: `2px solid ${isValid ? '#10b981' : THEME.accent}40`,\\n            borderRadius: 12,\\n            color: '#fff',\\n            textAlign: 'center',\\n            width: 220,\\n            outline: 'none'\\n          }}\\n        />\\n      </div>\\n\\n      {/* Voice Bar */}\\n      <div style={{\\n        width: '100%',\\n        padding: 16,\\n        background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n        borderRadius: 16,\\n        border: `2px solid ${isListening ? '#10b981' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'}`\\n      }}>\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10, marginBottom: 12 }}>\\n          <div style={{\\n            width: 10, height: 10, borderRadius: '50%',\\n            background: isListening ? '#10b981' : '#64748b',\\n            animation: isListening ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none'\\n          }} />\\n          <span style={{ color: '#06b6d4', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\n            \\ud83c\\udfa4 {isListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'READY'}\\n          </span>\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {isListening && (\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 3, height: 25, marginBottom: 10 }}>\\n            {[...Array(12)].map((_, i) => (\\n              <div key={i} style={{\\n                width: 3, background: 'linear-gradient(to top, #10b981, #06b6d4)',\\n                borderRadius: 2, animation: `wave 0.4s ${i * 0.05}s infinite alternate`, height: 8\\n              }} />\\n            ))}\\n          </div>\\n        )}\\n\\n        {transcript && (\\n          <div style={{ background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 8, padding: 10, marginBottom: 12 }}>\\n            <span style={{ color: '#10b981', fontSize: '0.75em' }}>\\u2713 HEARD</span>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', margin: '4px 0 0' }}>\\\"{transcript}\\\"</p>\\n          </div>\\n        )}\\n\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\\n          <button onClick={toggleListening} style={{\\n            padding: '10px 24px', borderRadius: 25, border: 'none',\\n            background: isListening ? '#ef4444' : '#10b981',\\n            color: 'white', fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer'\\n          }}>\\n            {isListening ? '\\u23f9\\ufe0f Stop' : '\\ud83c\\udfa4 Listen'}\\n          </button>\\n        </div>\\n      </div>\\n\\n      <button\\n        onClick={onNext}\\n        disabled={!isValid}\\n        style={{\\n          padding: '14px 40px',\\n          background: isValid ? THEME.accent : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\\n          border: 'none',\\n          borderRadius: 30,\\n          color: isValid ? '#000' : '#666',\\n          fontSize: '1em',\\n          fontWeight: 600,\\n          cursor: isValid ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed'\\n        }}\\n      >\\n        Send OTP \\u2192\\n      </button>\\n\\n      <style>{`\\n        @keyframes pulse { 0%,100%{opacity:1} 50%{opacity:0.5} }\\n        @keyframes wave { from{height:6px} to{height:20px} }\\n      `}</style>\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default BuilderPhone;\\nBUILDERPHONE\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udd22 STEP 3: Creating BuilderOTP.tsx...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$BUILDER_DIR/BuilderOTP.tsx\\\" << 'BUILDEROTP'\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from    speak(\\\"Please enter the 6-digit verification code.\\\");\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const handleChange = (value: string) => {\\n    const digits = value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 6);\\n    setLocalOtp(digits);\\n    onChange(digits);\\n  };\\n\\n  const isValid = localOtp.length === 6;\\n\\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => {\\n    if (p.length === 10) return `(${p.slice(0,3)}) {status === 'success' && (\\n          <>\\n            <div style={{ fontSize: '2.5em', marginBottom: 15 }}>\\u2705</div>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#10b981', fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Upload '\\ud83d\\udcc4'\\n};\\n\\nconst UniversalUploader: React.FC<Props> = ({\\n  accept = ['pdf', 'csv', 'xlsx', 'jpg', 'png', 'docx'],\\n  onUpload,\\n  speak,\\n  title = 'Upload Files',\\n  description = 'Drag & drop or click to upload',\\n  accentColor = '#B8860B'\\n}) => {\\n  const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);\\n  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);\\n  const [results, setResults] = useState<any[]>([]);\\n  const [dragActive, setDragActive] = useState(false);\\n  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\\n\\n  const acceptString = accept.map(ext => `.${ext}`).join(',');\\n\\n  const handleFiles = async (files: FileList | File[]) => {\\n    const fileArray = Array.from(files);\\n    if (fileArray.length === 0) return;\\n\\n URL.createObjectURL(file) : undefined\\n        });\\n      } catch (err: any) {\\n        uploadResults.push({ file, success: false, error: err.message });\\n      }\\n\\n      setProgress(Math.round(((i + 1) / fileArray.length) * 100));\\n    }\\n\\n    setResults(uploadResults);\\n    setUploading(false);\\n    onUpload(uploadResults);\\n\\n    const successCount = uploadResults.filter(r => r.success).length;\\n    speak?.(`Uploaded ${successCount} of ${fileArray.length} files`);\\n  };\\n\\n  const getIcon = (name: string) => FILE_ICONS[name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || ''] || '\\ud83d\\udcc4';\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div>\\n      <input\\n        ref={fileInputRef}\\n        type=\\\"file\\\"\\n        accept={acceptString}\\n        multiple\\n        onChange={e => e.target.files && handleFiles(e.target.files)}\\n        style={{ display: 'none' }}\\n      />\\n\\n      <div\\n        onDragEnter={() => setDragActive(true)}\\n        onDragLeave={() => setDragActive(false)}\\n        onDragOver={e => e.preventDefault()}\\n        onDrop={e => { e.preventDefault(); setDragActive(false); handleFiles(e.dataTransfer.files); }}\\n        onClick={() => !uploading && fileInputRef.current?.click()}\\n        style={{\\n          border: `2px dashed ${dragActive ? accentColor : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)'}`,\\n          borderRadius: 16,\\n          padding: '40px 20px',\\n          textAlign: 'center',\\n          cursor: uploading ? 'wait' : 'pointer',\\n          background: dragActive ? `${accentColor}20` : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',\\n          transition: 'all 0.3s'\\n        }}\\n      >\\n        {uploading ? (\\n          <>\\n            <div style={{ fontSize: '2.5em', marginBottom: 15 }}>\\ud83d\\udce4</div>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#06b6d4', margin: '0 0 15px' }}>Uploading... {progress}%</p>\\n            <div style={{ height: 8, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 4, maxWidth: 300, margin: '0 auto' }}>\\n              <div style={{ width: `${progress}%`, height: '100%', background: `linear-gradient(90deg, ${accentColor}, #06b6d4)`, borderRadius: 4 }} />\\n            </div>\\n          </>\\n        ) : (\\n          <>\\n            <div style={{ fontSize: '3em', marginBottom: 15 }}>{dragActive ? '\\ud83d\\udce5' : '\\ud83d\\udcc1'}</div>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', fontSize: '1.1em', margin: '0 0 8px' }}>{title}</p>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#64748b', fontSize: '0.85em', margin: 0 }}>{description}</p>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#64748b', fontSize: '0.75em', marginTop: 10 }}>\\n              Supports: {accept.map(e => e.toUpperCase()).join(', ')}\\n            </p>\\n          </>\\n        )}\\n      </div>\\n\\n      {results.length > 0 && (\\n        <div style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 10 }}>\\n            <span style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', fontSize: 14 }}>{results.length} files</span>\\n            <button onClick={() => setResults([])} style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#ef4444', cursor: 'pointer' }}>Clear</button>\\n          </div>\\n          {results.map((r, i) => (\\n            <div key={i} style={{\\n              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12,\\n              padding: '10px 14px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',\\n              borderRadius: 10, marginBottom: 8,\\n              border: `1px solid ${r.success ? \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udce4 PART 1: Creating UniversalUploader...\"\n\ncat > \"$COMMON_DIR/UniversalUploader.tsx\" << 'UNIVERSALUPLOADER'\nimport React, { useState, useRef } from 'react';\n\ninterface Props {\n  accept?: string[];\n  onUpload: (results: any[]) => void;\n  speak?: (t: string) => void;\n  title?: string;\n  description?: string;\n  accentColor?: string;\n}\n\nconst FILE_ICONS: Record<string, string> = {\n  pdf: '\ud83d\udcc4', csv: '\ud83d\udcca', xlsx: '\ud83d\udcd7', xls: '\ud83d\udcd7',\n  jpg: '\ud83d\uddbc\ufe0f', jpeg: '\ud83d\uddbc\ufe0f', png: '\ud83d\uddbc\ufe0f', useState(false);\n  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\n\n  const acceptString = accept.map(ext => `.${ext}`).join(',');\n\n  const handleFiles = async (files: FileList | File[]) => {\n    const fileArray = Array.from(files);\n    if (fileArray.length === 0) return;\n\n    setUploading(true);\n    setProgress(0);\n    speak?.(`Uploading ${fileArray.length} file${fileArray.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}`);\n\n    const uploadResults: any[] = [];\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < fileArray.length; i++) {\n      const file = fileArray[i];\n      const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || '';\n\n      try {\n        const formData = new FormData();\n        formData.append('file', file);\n        formData.append('fileType', ext);\n\n        const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/upload/file', {\n          method: 'POST',\n          body: formData\n        });\n\n        const data = await response.json();\n\n        uploadResults.push({\n          file,\n          success: response.ok,\n          data,\n          preview: ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif'].includes(ext) ? URL.createObjectURL(file) : undefined\n        });\n      } catch (err: any) {\n        uploadResults.push({ file, success: false, error: err.message });\n      }\n\n      setProgress(Math.round(((i + 1) / fileArray.length) * 100));\n    }\n\n    setResults(uploadResults);\n    setUploading(false);\n    onUpload(uploadResults);\n\n    const successCount = uploadResults.filter(r => r.success).length;\n    speak?.(`Uploaded ${successCount} of ${fileArray.length} files`);\n  };\n\n  const getIcon = (name: string) => FILE_ICONS[name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || ''] || '\ud83d\udcc4';\n\n  return (\n    <div>\n      <input\n        ref={fileInputRef}\n        type=\"file\"\n        accept={acceptString}\n        multiple\n        onChange={e => e.target.files && handleFiles(e.target.files)}\n        style={{ display: 'none' }}\n      />\n\n      <div\n        onDragEnter={() => setDragActive(true)}\n        onDragLeave={() => setDragActive(false)}\n        onDragOver={e => e.preventDefault()}\n        onDrop={e => { e.preventDefault(); setDragActive(false); handleFiles(e.dataTransfer.files); }}\n        onClick={() => !uploading && fileInputRef.current?.click()}\n        style={{\n          border: `2px dashed ${dragActive ? accentColor : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)'}`,\n          borderRadius: 16,\n          padding: '40px 20px',\n          textAlign: 'center',\n          cursor: uploading ? '\ud83d\udce5' : '\ud83d\udcc1'}</div>\n            <p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', fontSize: '1.1em', margin: '0 0 8px' }}>{title}</p>\n            <p style={{ color: '#64748b', fontSize: '0.85em', margin: 0 }}>{description}</p>\n            <p style={{ color: '#64748b', fontSize: '0.75em', marginTop: 10 }}>\n              Supports: {accept.map(e => e.toUpperCase()).join(', ')}\n            </p>\n          </>\n        )}\n      </div>\n\n      {results.length > 0 && (\n        <div style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 10 }}>\n            <span style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', fontSize: 14 }}>{results.length} files</span>\n            <button onClick={() => setResults([])} style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#ef4444', cursor: 'pointer' }}>Clear</button>\n          </div>\n          {results.map((r, i) => (\n            <div key={i} style={{\n              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12,\n              padding: '10px 14px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',\n              borderRadius: 10, marginBottom: 8,\n              border: `1px solid ${r.success ? \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udce4 PART 1: Creating UniversalUploader...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$COMMON_DIR/UniversalUploader.tsx\\\" << 'UNIVERSALUPLOADER'\\nimport React, { useState, useRef } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface Props {\\n  accept?: string[];\\n  onUpload: (results: any[]) => void;\\n  speak?: (t: string) => void;\\n  title?: string;\\n  description?: string;\\n  accentColor?: string;\\n}\\n\\nconst FILE_ICONS: Record<string, string> = {\\n  pdf: '\\ud83d\\udcc4', csv: '\\ud83d\\udcca', xlsx: '\\ud83d\\udcd7', xls: '\\ud83d\\udcd7',\\n  jpg: '\\ud83d\\uddbc\\ufe0f', jpeg: '\\ud83d\\uddbc\\ufe0f', png: '\\ud83d\\uddbc\\ufe0f', gif: '\\ud83d\\uddbc\\ufe0f',\\n  docx: '\\ud83d\\udcdd', doc: '\\ud83d\\udcdd', json: '\\ud83d\\udccb', xml: '\\ud83d\\udccb', txt: '\\ud83d\\udcc4'\\n};\\n\\nconst UniversalUploader: React.FC<Props> = ({\\n  accept = ['pdf', 'csv', 'xlsx', 'jpg', 'png', 'docx'],\\n  onUpload,\\n  speak,\\n  title = 'Upload Files',\\n  description = 'Drag & drop or click to upload',\\n  accentColor = '#B8860B'\\n}) => {\\n  const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);\\n  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);\\n  const [results, setResults] = useState<any[]>([]);\\n  const [dragActive, setDragActive] = useState(false);\\n  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\\n\\n  const acceptString = accept.map(ext => `.${ext}`).join(',');\\n\\n  const handleFiles = async (files: FileList | File[]) => {\\n    const fileArray = Array.from(files);\\n    if (fileArray.length === 0) return;\\n\\n    setUploading(true);\\n    setProgress(0);\\n    speak?.(`Uploading ${fileArray.length} file${fileArray.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}`);\\n\\n    const uploadResults: any[] = [];\\n\\n    for (let i = 0; i < fileArray.length; i++) {\\n      const file = fileArray[i];\\n      const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || '';\\n\\n      try {\\n        const formData = new FormData();\\n        formData.append('file', file);\\n        formData.append('fileType', ext);\\n\\n        const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/upload/file', {\\n          method: 'POST',\\n          body: formData\\n        });\\n\\n        const data = await response.json();\\n\\n        uploadResults.push({\\n          file,\\n          success: response.ok,\\n          data,\\n          preview: ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif'].includes(ext) ? URL.createObjectURL(file) : undefined\\n        });\\n      } catch (err: any) {\\n        uploadResults.push({ file, success: false, error: err.message });\\n      }\\n\\n      setProgress(Math.round(((i + 1) / fileArray.length) * 100));\\n    }\\n\\n    setResults(uploadResults);\\n    setUploading(false);\\n    onUpload(uploadResults);\\n\\n    const successCount = uploadResults.filter(r => r.success).length;\\n    speak?.(`Uploaded ${successCount} of ${fileArray.length} files`);\\n  };\\n\\n  const getIcon = (name: string) => FILE_ICONS[name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || ''] || '\\ud83d\\udcc4';\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div>\\n      <input\\n        ref={fileInputRef}\\n        type=\\\"file\\\"\\n        accept={acceptString}\\n        multiple\\n        onChange={e => e.target.files && handleFiles(e.target.files)}\\n        style={{ display: 'none' }}\\n      />\\n\\n      <div\\n        onDragEnter={() => setDragActive(true)}\\n        onDragLeave={() => setDragActive(false)}\\n        onDragOver={e => e.preventDefault()}\\n        onDrop={e => { e.preventDefault(); setDragActive(false); handleFiles(e.dataTransfer.files); }}\\n        onClick={() => !uploading && fileInputRef.current?.click()}\\n        style={{\\n          border: `2px dashed ${dragActive ? accentColor : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)'}`,\\n          borderRadius: 16,\\n          padding: '40px 20px',\\n          textAlign: 'center',\\n          cursor: uploading ? 'wait' : 'pointer',\\n          background: dragActive ? `${accentColor}20` : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',\\n          transition: 'all 0.3s'\\n        }}\\n      >\\n        {uploading ? (\\n          <>\\n            <div style={{ fontSize: '2.5em', marginBottom: 15 }}>\\ud83d\\udce4</div>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#06b6d4', margin: '0 0 15px' }}>Uploading... {progress}%</p>\\n            <div style={{ height: 8, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 4, maxWidth: 300, margin: '0 auto' }}>\\n              <div style={{ width: `${progress}%`, height: '100%', background: `linear-gradient(90deg, ${accentColor}, #06b6d4)`, borderRadius: 4 }} />\\n            </div>\\n          </>\\n        ) : (\\n          <>\\n            <div style={{ fontSize: '3em', marginBottom: 15 }}>{dragActive ? '\\ud83d\\udce5' : '\\ud83d\\udcc1'}</div>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', fontSize: '1.1em', margin: '0 0 8px' }}>{title}</p>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#64748b', fontSize: '0.85em', margin: 0 }}>{description}</p>\\n            <p style={{ color: '#64748b', fontSize: '0.75em', marginTop: 10 }}>\\n              Supports: {accept.map(e => e.toUpperCase()).join(', ')}\\n            </p>\\n          </>\\n        )}\\n      </div>\\n\\n      {results.length > 0 && (\\n        <div style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 10 }}>\\n            <span style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', fontSize: 14 }}>{results.length} files</span>\\n            <button onClick={() => setResults([])} style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#ef4444', cursor: 'pointer' }}>Clear</button>\\n          </div>\\n          {results.map((r, i) => (\\n            <div key={i} style={{\\n              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12,\\n              padding: '10px 14px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',\\n              borderRadius: 10, marginBottom: 8,\\n              border: `1px solid ${r.success ?
